–ü–†–û–ú–¢ 26 - —Ä–æ–º–∞—à–∫–∏ –Ω–∞ –ª–∏—Ü–µ + –±–µ–ª—ã–π —Ñ–æ–Ω üíõ

Edit and enhance your photo without changing color correction or adding filters. Do not add filters to your photo. Do not change color correction. Do not touch, alter, or blur your face. Make your face textured and high-quality. Preserve all facial features. Add freckles to your face. Create a high-quality photo. Do not change your face or lip color.
Eye, eyelash, and eyebrow fixation:
DO NOT alter the eyes, eyelids, irises, sclera, or eye shape.
DO NOT alter the length, curl, thickness, direction, or style of eyelashes.
Eyelashes must remain exactly as in the original photo.
DO NOT alter the shape, color, direction, or arch of eyebrows.
Eyebrows must remain exactly as in the original photo.
Remove imperfections to create beautiful, textured, and slightly shiny skin.
Place daisies of different sizes on your face for a realistic look. Arrange them randomly. Enhance the photo to 8K quality. Change the background to a nice white background. Don't change the photo filter.
